<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spelonk.html>spelonk</a> (79430)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spelonke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">spelonque</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">spelonca</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">spelunca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cave, cavern; grotto; den</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σπῆλυγξ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spêlunx</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σπέος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spéos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cave, cavern</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">sperzie</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">asparagus</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">boon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bean</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, named after its use along with asparagus in dishes.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A variety of <span class="Latn" lang="en">green bean</span>, <i>Phaseolus <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></i>, with seeds that have not fully matured.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">slaboon</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***sphinx.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sphinx.html>sphinx</a> (40156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/Sphinx_of_Gizeh.jpg/220px-Sphinx_of_Gizeh.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/Sphinx_of_Gizeh.jpg/330px-Sphinx_of_Gizeh.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/Sphinx_of_Gizeh.jpg/440px-Sphinx_of_Gizeh.jpg 2x" data-file-width="450" data-file-height="337" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>The great <a href = vnd.unilang:sphinx.html>Sphinx</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:giza.html>Giza</a></div></div></div>
<div>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">Spynx</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:sphinx.html>Sphinx</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Σφίγξ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Sphínx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, perhaps from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σφίγγω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sphíngō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to squeeze, to strangle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Egyptian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Egyptian language">Egyptian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="egy"> </td></tr></tbody></table></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="egy-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><i class="Latinx mention" lang="egy">šzp-ꜥnḫ</i></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">divine image</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, literally "living image".</div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sphinx.html>sphinx</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">sphinxes</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">sphinges</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A creature with the head of a person and the body of an animal (commonly a lion).
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Shelley and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>Sculptured on <a href = vnd.unilang:alabaster.html>alabaster</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:obelisk.html>obelisk</a>, / Or <a href = vnd.unilang:jasper.html>jasper</a> tomb, or mutilated <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sphinx.html>sphinx</a></b><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A person who keeps his/her thoughts and intentions secret; an enigmatic person.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mandrill, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Mandrillus_sphinx" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Mandrillus sphinx"><i>Mandrillus <a href = vnd.unilang:sphinx.html>sphinx</a></i></a></span>, formerly classified a baboon, and called <a href = vnd.unilang:sphinx.html>sphinx</a> baboon.</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:sphinx.html>sphinx</a> moth.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A sphincter.
<ul><li><b>1982</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lawrence_Durrell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lawrence Durrell">Lawrence Durrell</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:constance.html>Constance</a></i>, Faber amp; Faber 2004 (<i>Avignon Quintet</i>), page 836:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:constance.html>Constance</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> boastfully, ‘My <b>sphinxes</b> are strong and in good repair. I <i>order</i> you to come.’</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">person who keeps his/her thoughts and intentions secret</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">enigma</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sphinx.html>sphinx</a> moth</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">sphingian</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sphinx.html>sphinx</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">sphinxes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">sphinxing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">sphinxed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To decorate with sphinxes
<dl><dd><i>a marble <b>sphinxed</b> chimney-piece</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>To adopt the posture of the <a href = vnd.unilang:sphinx.html>Sphinx</a>.
<dl><dd><i>A hot lion with a very bloated stomach ... will adopt either a <b>sphinxed</b> or a squatting posture which <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> some of the weight off its belly.</i></dd>
<dd><i>Several animals maintained either a crouched ... or a <b>sphinxing</b> posture (abdomen on the floor)</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>To be inscrutable, often through silence
<dl><dd>(<b>1900</b>) <i>The <b>sphinxèd</b> riddle of the Universe / Nature's unsolved enigma, who may prove?</i></dd>
<dd>(<b>1933</b>) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:janet.html>Janet</a> Gaynor, so they tell, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>sphinxing</b> it and <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a> into a Retirement, with "Nothing to Say — Please Go Away" written on the doormat.</i></dd>
<dd>(<b>1934</b>) <i>The <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> of science will climb grassy hillsides of [<a href = vnd.unilang:easter.html>Easter</a>] island to peer at hundreds of great stone <a href = vnd.unilang:faces.html>faces</a> that have so far out-<b>sphinxed</b> the <a href = vnd.unilang:sphinx.html>sphinx</a> in determined silence about the past.</i></dd>
<dd>(<b>1954</b>) <i>"What are you two <b>sphinxing</b> about?" <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> Jessica, but her husband <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> Never mind</i></dd>
<dd>(<b>1964</b>) <i>What with Fisher whole-hogging on one side, and K. of K. <b>sphinxing</b> on the other, Churchill <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> his work cut out to get any sort of agreement at all.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>To make one guess at the unknowable
<dl><dd>(<b>1933</b>) <i>Perhaps Nature <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>sphinxing</b> us on purpose. Whatever her <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> may be, perhaps she <a href = vnd.unilang:gets.html>gets</a> her work done better when she appeals to our gambling <a href = vnd.unilang:instincts.html>instincts</a>. If you <a href = vnd.unilang:knew.html>knew</a> for certain exactly how your marriage <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> going to turn out ...</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>To befuddle
<dl><dd>(<b>2010</b>) <i>She swiveled and <b>sphinxed</b> Giles. 'And you, I suppose you've never <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> here either?' Giles squirmed. 'Well, I – that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, Miss Wh—, I mean, Miss <a href = vnd.unilang:taylor.html>Taylor</a>, I –' He looked to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> for rescue.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>For the feminine to co-opt, dominate, or devour the masculine, especially from a paranoid fear of this happening
<dl><dd>(<b>1986</b>) <i>modernism's fears of being <b>sphinxed</b> by a feminized mass culture</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr />
</body>

***spier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spier.html>spier</a> (12128)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:spier.html>spier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pointed object; blade of grass; long pole; muscle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*spīr</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*spīraz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*spīrǭ</i>. In Middle Dutch, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> the meaning "muscle", likely due to the similarities in shape between its earlier meanings and muscle fibers.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spier.html>spier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spieren.html>spieren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spiertje.html>spiertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>muscle (contractile tissue)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> blade (of a plant)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spriet.html>spriet</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:halm.html>halm</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> blade of grass
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grasspriet.html>grasspriet</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">grashalm</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>spar (pole)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">rondhout</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">armspier</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">beenspier</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">buikspier</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bilspier</span></li>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">oogspier</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gespierd.html>gespierd</a></span></li>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">spierversterken</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spier.html>spier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the collective of muscles</li>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:spier.html>spier</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spiesse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">spiez</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">spioz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*speutaz</i>. Cognate to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">spit</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">spiet</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spijker.html>spijker</a> (10101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Nail.agr.jpg/220px-Nail.agr.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="244" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Nail.agr.jpg/330px-Nail.agr.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Nail.agr.jpg/440px-Nail.agr.jpg 2x" data-file-width="691" data-file-height="767" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:spijker.html>spijker</a></div></div></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spiker</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*spīkō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stick, splinter, point</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*spey-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be pointed; sharp point, stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spijker.html>spijker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spijkers.html>spijkers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spijker.html>spijkertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spīker</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*spīkāri</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*spīkārī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">spīcārium</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Speicher</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">spīkari</i>.
</p>

***spijkerbroek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spijkerbroek.html>spijkerbroek</a> (15117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spijker.html>spijker</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nail (metal fastener)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:broek.html>broek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trousers, <a href = vnd.unilang:pants.html>pants</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Named after the use of rivets in <a href = vnd.unilang:jeans.html>jeans</a>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> thought to resemble the heads of <a href = vnd.unilang:nails.html>nails</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spijkerbroek.html>spijkerbroek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spijkerbroeken.html>spijkerbroeken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spijkerbroek.html>spijkerbroekje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pair of <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jeans.html>jeans</a></span>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Not used in <span class="Latn" lang="en">Flanders</span>, where the loanword <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jeans.html>jeans</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used instead.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jeans.html>jeans</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">texasbroek</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">spijkerstof</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:spijkerbroek.html>spijkerbroek</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

***spijs.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spijs.html>spijs</a> (50665)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spise</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">spīsa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">spesa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spijs.html>spijs</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spijzen.html>spijzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spijs.html>spijsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>foodstuff in general
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tafel.html>tafel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedekt.html>gedekt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:allerlei.html>allerlei</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heerlijke.html>heerlijke</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:spijzen.html>spijzen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The table <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> arranged with all <a href = vnd.unilang:kinds.html>kinds</a> of delicious <b>foods</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>almond paste; <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> almond paste surrogate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brood.html>brood</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bevat.html>bevat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:spijs.html>spijs</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This bread contains <b>almond paste</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:spijs.html>spijs</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vloeien.html>vloeien</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zodat.html>zodat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mallen.html>mallen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:landt.html>landt</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>almond paste</b> must flow, in order for it to <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> in the molds.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> one of a number of historically feminine nouns that have undergone masculinisation in Belgian Dutch. It <a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a> feminine in (very) formal Netherlands Dutch.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">despijt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">despit</i> (from which also English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">despite</i>). The first syllable <i>de-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> interpreted as a definite article ("<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spijt.html>spijt</a>") and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> then dropped.

***spijten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spijten.html>spijten</a> (14500)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spiten</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spijt.html>spijt</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spijten.html>spijten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause regret to, to cause to be <a href = vnd.unilang:sorry.html>sorry</a>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daden.html>daden</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:spijten.html>speten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>He <b>regretted</b> his <a href = vnd.unilang:deeds.html>deeds</a>. (His <a href = vnd.unilang:deeds.html>deeds</a> <b>caused</b> him <b>regret</b>.)</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to regret, to be <a href = vnd.unilang:sorry.html>sorry</a>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:spijt.html>spijt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>I <b>regret</b> it.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Usually, no explicit subject <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> given, and the verb <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used impersonally with the dummy pronoun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i>, in the sense that something <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> "being the regret to one" or "it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> one's regret", which could be rendered in English as "It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> my regret...".
</p>

***spinazie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spinazie.html>spinazie</a> (17447)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spinagie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">espinache</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">spinachium</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Spanish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Spanish">Old Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osp">espinaca</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">إسفاناخ</i> | , from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">اسفناج</i> | .
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spinazie.html>spinazie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spinazie.html>spinazies</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>spinach (a particular edible plant, <i>Spinacia oleracea</i>)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:spinnen.html>spinnen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*spinnan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*spinnaną</i>.

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spits.html>spits</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afbijten.html>afbijten</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Spitze</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spits.html>spits</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spitsen.html>spitsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spits.html>spitsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A top, a peak, a pinnacle or an apex.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A spire.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A striker (both the position and the player), often referring to the centre forward.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A frontline battalion, a front subdivision of a vanguard.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">spire</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:torenspits.html>torenspits</a></span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_3">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spitsuur.html>spitsuur</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:torenspits.html>torenspits</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Backformation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spitsuur.html>spitsuur</a></i>, but especially <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">avondspits</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ochtendspits</i>, which are themselves shortenings from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">avondspitsuur</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ochtendspitsuur</i>. Around 1940 the term <i><a href = vnd.unilang:spits.html>spits</a></i> (“peak”, etymology 2) <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> also commonly used for annual peak traffic during the summer holiday, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> another likely influence for the shortened form. The use of the article <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i> (earlier used for <i>avondspits</i> and <i>ochtendspits</i>) rather than <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> (used for <i><a href = vnd.unilang:spitsuur.html>spitsuur</a></i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> influenced by etymology 2.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spits.html>spits</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spitsen.html>spitsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spits.html>spitsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>rush hour <span class="defdate">[from mid 20th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spitsuur.html>spitsuur</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:splijten.html>splijten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to split</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spleet.html>spleet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spleten.html>spleten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spleetje.html>spleetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>crack, cleft, split</li>
<li>fissure, slit</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spliten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*splītan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*splītaną</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">spleißen</i>, West Frisian and Danish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:splitte.html>splitte</a></i>, English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">split</i> (borrowed from Middle Dutch).
</p>
